Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

TestNamespaceScopedEvaluation(t *testing.T) {\n\ttestStore := setupTestDatabase(t)\n\tdefer testStore.Shutdown(context.Background())\n\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tstore, err := storagesql.New(testStore.DB)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create two namespaces\n\t_, err = store.CreateNamespace(ctx, &flipt.CreateNamespaceRequest{\n\t\tKey: \"namespace-1\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t_, err = store.CreateNamespace(ctx, &flipt.CreateNamespaceRequest{\n\t\tKey: \"namespace-2\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create flag in namespace-1\n\t_, err = store.CreateFlag(ctx, &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"namespace-1\",\n\t\tKey:          \"shared-flag\",\n\t\tName:         \"Shared Flag\",\n\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,\n\t\tEnabled:      true,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create flag in namespace-2 with different name\n\t_, err = store.CreateFlag(ctx, &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"namespace-2\",\n\t\tKey:          \"shared-flag\",\n\t\tName:         \"Different Flag\",\n\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,\n\t\tEnabled:      false,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create evaluation server\n\tlogger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)\n\tserver := evaluation.New(logger, store)\n\n\t// Create HTTP server\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\tregisterEvaluationHandlers(mux, server)\n\tts := httptest.NewServer(mux)\n\tdefer ts.Close()\n\n\t// Evaluate in namespace-1\n\treq1 := rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"namespace-1\",\n\t\tFlagKey:      \"shared-flag\",\n\t\tEntityId:     \"user-123\",\n\t}\n\tdata1, err := protojson.Marshal(&req1)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tresp1, err := http.Post(ts.URL+\"/evaluate/v1/boolean\", \"application/json\", bytes.NewReader(data1))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdefer resp1.Body.Close()\n\n\tbody1, err := io.ReadAll(resp1.Body)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar result1 rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse\n\terr = protojson.Unmarshal(body1, &result1)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Evaluate in namespace-2\n\treq2 := rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"namespace-2\",\n\t\tFlagKey:      \"shared-flag\",\n\t\tEntityId:     \"user-123\",\n\t}\n\tdata2, err := protojson.Marshal(&req2)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tresp2, err := http.Post(ts.URL+\"/evaluate/v1/boolean\", \"application/json\", bytes.NewReader(data2))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdefer resp2.Body.Close()\n\n\tbody2, err := io.ReadAll(resp2.Body)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar result2 rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse\n\terr = protojson.Unmarshal(body2, &result2)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Assert different results for same flag key in different namespaces\n\tassert.True(t, result1.Enabled)\n\tassert.False(t, result2.Enabled)\n}\n\n// TestInvalidRequestBody tests handling of invalid JSON request\nfunc TestInvalidRequestBody(t *testing.T) TestBatchEvaluationSuccess(t *testing.T) {\n\ttestStore := setupTestDatabase(t)\n\tdefer testStore.Shutdown(context.Background())\n\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tstore, err := storagesql.New(testStore.DB)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create namespace\n\t_, err = store.CreateNamespace(ctx, &flipt.CreateNamespaceRequest{\n\t\tKey: \"default\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create boolean flag\n\t_, err = store.CreateFlag(ctx, &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"default\",\n\t\tKey:          \"flag-1\",\n\t\tName:         \"Flag 1\",\n\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,\n\t\tEnabled:      true,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create variant flag\n\t_, err = store.CreateFlag(ctx, &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"default\",\n\t\tKey:          \"flag-2\",\n\t\tName:         \"Flag 2\",\n\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType_VARIANT_FLAG_TYPE,\n\t\tEnabled:      true,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create a variant\n\t_, err = store.CreateVariant(ctx, &flipt.CreateVariantRequest{\n\t\tNamespaceKey: \"default\",\n\t\tFlagKey:      \"flag-2\",\n\t\tKey:          \"variant-a\",\n\t\tName:         \"Variant A\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create evaluation server\n\tlogger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)\n\tserver := evaluation.New(logger, store)\n\n\t// Create HTTP server\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\tregisterEvaluationHandlers(mux, server)\n\tts := httptest.NewServer(mux)\n\tdefer ts.Close()\n\n\t// Make batch request\n\tbatchReq := rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest{\n\t\tRequestId: \"batch-1\",\n\t\tRequests: []*rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: \"default\",\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      \"flag-1\",\n\t\t\t\tEntityId:     \"user-1\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: \"default\",\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      \"flag-2\",\n\t\t\t\tEntityId:     \"user-1\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tbatchData, err := protojson.Marshal(&batchReq)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tresp, err := http.Post(\n\t\tts.URL+\"/evaluate/v1/batch\",\n\t\t\"application/json\",\n\t\tbytes.NewReader(batchData),\n\t)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n\n\trequire.Equal(t, http.StatusOK, resp.StatusCode)\n\n\trespData, err := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar batchResp rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse\n\terr = protojson.Unmarshal(respData, &batchResp)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Assert we have responses for both requests\n\tassert.Len(t, batchResp.Responses, 2)\n\n\t// First response should be boolean\n\tassert.Equal(t, rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, batchResp.Responses[0].Type)\n\tboolResp := batchResp.Responses[0].GetBooleanResponse()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, boolResp)\n\tassert.True(t, boolResp.Enabled)\n\tassert.Equal(t, \"flag-1\", boolResp.FlagKey)\n\n\t// Second response should be variant\n\tassert.Equal(t, rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE, batchResp.Responses[1].Type)\n\tvariantResp := batchResp.Responses[1].GetVariantResponse()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, variantResp)\n\tassert.Equal(t, \"flag-2\", variantResp.FlagKey)\n}\n\n// TestBatchEvaluationWithMissingFlag tests batch evaluation when one flag doesn't exist\nfunc setupTestDatabase creates and initializes a test database\nfunc setupTestDatabase(t *testing.T) *sqltesting.Database {\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\ttestDB, err := sqltesting.Open()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, testDB)\n\n\treturn testDB\n}\n\n// registerEvaluationHandlers registers the evaluation service handlers to an HTTP mux\nfunc registerEvaluationHandlers(mux *http.ServeMux, server *evaluation.Server) {\n\t// Boolean evaluation endpoint\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/boolean\", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest\n\t\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to read request body\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer r.Body.Close()\n\n\t\tif err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to unmarshal request\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 5*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tresp, err := server.Boolean(ctx, &req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"evaluation error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\trespData, err := protojson.Marshal(resp)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to marshal response\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t_, _ = w.Write(respData)\n\t})\n\n\t// Variant evaluation endpoint\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/variant\", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest\n\t\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to read request body\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer r.Body.Close()\n\n\t\tif err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to unmarshal request\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 5*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tresp, err := server.Variant(ctx, &req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"evaluation error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\trespData, err := protojson.Marshal(resp)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"failed to marshal response\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", package integration

import (
	"bytes"

// TestBooleanEvaluationSuccess tests the boolean evaluation endpoint with a valid request
func TestBooleanEvaluationSuccess(t *testing.T) {
	testStore := setupTestDatabase(t)
	defer testStore.Shutdown(context.Background())

	// Create test data
	ctx := context.Background()
	store, err := storagesql.New(testStore.DB)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Create namespace
	_, err = store.CreateNamespace(ctx, &flipt.CreateNamespaceRequest{
		Key: "default",
	})
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Create boolean flag
	flag, err := store.CreateFlag(ctx, &flipt.CreateFlagRequest{
		NamespaceKey: "default",
		Key:          "feature-enabled",
		Name:         "Feature Enabled",
		Type:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
		Enabled:      true,
	})
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, flag)

	// Create evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	server := evaluation.New(logger, store)

	// Create HTTP server using httptest
	mux := http.NewServeMux()
	registerEvaluationHandlers(mux, server)
	ts := httptest.NewServer(mux)
	defer ts.Close()

	// Make request
	reqBody := rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest{
		NamespaceKey: "default",
		FlagKey:      "feature-enabl
